\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{Introduction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{============}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ is\ a\ single\ file\ library.\ To\ use\ it,\ do\ something\ like\ the\ following\ in\ one\ .c\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ DR\_WAV\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#include\ "{}dr\_wav.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ then\ \#include\ this\ file\ in\ other\ parts\ of\ the\ program\ as\ you\ would\ with\ any\ other\ header\ file.\ Do\ something\ like\ the\ following\ to\ read\ audio\ data:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\ wav;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ (!drwav\_init\_file(\&wav,\ "{}my\_song.wav"{},\ NULL))\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Error\ opening\ WAV\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_int32*\ pDecodedInterleavedPCMFrames\ =\ malloc(wav.totalPCMFrameCount\ *\ wav.channels\ *\ sizeof(drwav\_int32));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ size\_t\ numberOfSamplesActuallyDecoded\ =\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32(\&wav,\ wav.totalPCMFrameCount,\ pDecodedInterleavedPCMFrames);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_uninit(\&wav);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{If\ you\ just\ want\ to\ quickly\ open\ and\ read\ the\ audio\ data\ in\ a\ single\ operation\ you\ can\ do\ something\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ unsigned\ int\ channels;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ unsigned\ int\ sampleRate;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_uint64\ totalPCMFrameCount;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ float*\ pSampleData\ =\ drwav\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32("{}my\_song.wav"{},\ \&channels,\ \&sampleRate,\ \&totalPCMFrameCount,\ NULL);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ (pSampleData\ ==\ NULL)\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Error\ opening\ and\ reading\ WAV\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_free(pSampleData,\ NULL);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ examples\ above\ use\ versions\ of\ the\ API\ that\ convert\ the\ audio\ data\ to\ a\ consistent\ format\ (32-\/bit\ signed\ PCM,\ in\ this\ case),\ but\ you\ can\ still\ output\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{audio\ data\ in\ its\ internal\ format\ (see\ notes\ below\ for\ supported\ formats):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ size\_t\ framesRead\ =\ drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames(\&wav,\ wav.totalPCMFrameCount,\ pDecodedInterleavedPCMFrames);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ also\ read\ the\ raw\ bytes\ of\ audio\ data,\ which\ could\ be\ useful\ if\ dr\_wav\ does\ not\ have\ native\ support\ for\ a\ particular\ data\ format:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ size\_t\ bytesRead\ =\ drwav\_read\_raw(\&wav,\ bytesToRead,\ pRawDataBuffer);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{dr\_wav\ can\ also\ be\ used\ to\ output\ WAV\ files.\ This\ does\ not\ currently\ support\ compressed\ formats.\ To\ use\ this,\ look\ at\ \`{}drwav\_init\_write()`,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\`{}drwav\_init\_file\_write()`,\ etc.\ Use\ \`{}drwav\_write\_pcm\_frames()`\ to\ write\ samples,\ or\ \`{}drwav\_write\_raw()`\ to\ write\ raw\ data\ in\ the\ "{}data"{}\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_data\_format\ format;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.container\ =\ drwav\_container\_riff;\ \ \ \ \ //\ <-\/-\/\ drwav\_container\_riff\ =\ normal\ WAV\ files,\ drwav\_container\_w64\ =\ Sony\ Wave64.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.format\ =\ DR\_WAVE\_FORMAT\_PCM;\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ <-\/-\/\ Any\ of\ the\ DR\_WAVE\_FORMAT\_*\ codes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.channels\ =\ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.sampleRate\ =\ 44100;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ format.bitsPerSample\ =\ 16;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_init\_file\_write(\&wav,\ "{}data/recording.wav"{},\ \&format,\ NULL);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drwav\_uint64\ framesWritten\ =\ drwav\_write\_pcm\_frames(pWav,\ frameCount,\ pSamples);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{Note\ that\ writing\ to\ AIFF\ or\ RIFX\ is\ not\ supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{dr\_wav\ has\ support\ for\ decoding\ from\ a\ number\ of\ different\ encapsulation\ formats.\ See\ below\ for\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{Build\ Options}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{=============}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ these\ options\ before\ including\ this\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ DR\_WAV\_NO\_CONVERSION\_API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Disables\ conversion\ APIs\ such\ as\ \`{}drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()`\ and\ \`{}drwav\_s16\_to\_f32()`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ DR\_WAV\_NO\_STDIO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Disables\ APIs\ that\ initialize\ a\ decoder\ from\ a\ file\ such\ as\ \`{}drwav\_init\_file()`,\ \`{}drwav\_init\_file\_write()`,\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ DR\_WAV\_NO\_WCHAR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Disables\ all\ functions\ ending\ with\ \`{}\_w`.\ Use\ this\ if\ your\ compiler\ does\ not\ provide\ wchar.h.\ Not\ required\ if\ DR\_WAV\_NO\_STDIO\ is\ also\ defined.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{Supported\ Encapsulations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{========================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ RIFF\ (Regular\ WAV)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ RIFX\ (Big-\/Endian)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ AIFF\ (Does\ not\ currently\ support\ ADPCM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ RF64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ W64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{Note\ that\ AIFF\ and\ RIFX\ do\ not\ support\ write\ mode,\ nor\ do\ they\ support\ reading\ of\ metadata.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{Supported\ Encodings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{===================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Unsigned\ 8-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Signed\ 12-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Signed\ 16-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Signed\ 24-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Signed\ 32-\/bit\ PCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ IEEE\ 32-\/bit\ floating\ point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ IEEE\ 64-\/bit\ floating\ point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ A-\/law\ and\ u-\/law}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Microsoft\ ADPCM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ IMA\ ADPCM\ (DVI,\ format\ code\ 0x11)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{8-\/bit\ PCM\ encodings\ are\ always\ assumed\ to\ be\ unsigned.\ Signed\ 8-\/bit\ encoding\ can\ only\ be\ read\ with\ \`{}drwav\_read\_raw()`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{Note\ that\ ADPCM\ is\ not\ currently\ supported\ with\ AIFF.\ Contributions\ welcome.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{Notes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{=====}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ Samples\ are\ always\ interleaved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ The\ default\ read\ function\ does\ not\ do\ any\ data\ conversion.\ Use\ \`{}drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()`,\ \`{}drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s32()`\ and\ \`{}drwav\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ to\ read\ and\ convert\ audio\ data\ to\ 32-\/bit\ floating\ point,\ signed\ 32-\/bit\ integer\ and\ signed\ 16-\/bit\ integer\ samples\ respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_wav\ will\ try\ to\ read\ the\ WAV\ file\ as\ best\ it\ can,\ even\ if\ it's\ not\ strictly\ conformant\ to\ the\ WAV\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00423\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00424\ \textcolor{comment}{Callback\ for\ when\ drwav\_init\_ex()\ finds\ a\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00425\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00426\ \textcolor{comment}{pChunkUserData\ \ \ \ [in]\ The\ user\ data\ that\ was\ passed\ to\ the\ pChunkUserData\ parameter\ of\ drwav\_init\_ex()\ and\ family.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00431\ \textcolor{comment}{container\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [in]\ Whether\ or\ not\ the\ WAV\ file\ is\ a\ RIFF\ or\ Wave64\ container.\ If\ you're\ unsure\ of\ the\ difference,\ assume\ RIFF.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00432\ \textcolor{comment}{pFMT\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ [in]\ A\ pointer\ to\ the\ object\ containing\ the\ contents\ of\ the\ "{}fmt"{}\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00433\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00434\ \textcolor{comment}{Returns\ the\ number\ of\ bytes\ read\ +\ seeked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00435\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00436\ \textcolor{comment}{To\ read\ data\ from\ the\ chunk,\ call\ onRead(),\ passing\ in\ pReadSeekUserData\ as\ the\ first\ parameter.\ Do\ the\ same\ for\ seeking\ with\ onSeek().\ The\ return\ value\ must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00437\ \textcolor{comment}{be\ the\ total\ number\ of\ bytes\ you\ have\ read\ \_plus\_\ seeked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00438\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00439\ \textcolor{comment}{Use\ the\ \`{}container`\ argument\ to\ discriminate\ the\ fields\ in\ \`{}pChunkHeader-\/>id`.\ If\ the\ container\ is\ \`{}drwav\_container\_riff`\ or\ \`{}drwav\_container\_rf64`\ you\ should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00440\ \textcolor{comment}{use\ \`{}id.fourcc`,\ otherwise\ you\ should\ use\ \`{}id.guid`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00441\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00442\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ \`{}pFMT`\ parameter\ can\ be\ used\ to\ determine\ the\ data\ format\ of\ the\ wave\ file.\ Use\ \`{}drwav\_fmt\_get\_format()`\ to\ get\ the\ sample\ format,\ which\ will\ be\ one\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00443\ \textcolor{comment}{\`{}DR\_WAVE\_FORMAT\_*\`{}\ identifiers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00444\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00445\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ read\ pointer\ will\ be\ sitting\ on\ the\ first\ byte\ after\ the\ chunk's\ header.\ You\ must\ not\ attempt\ to\ read\ beyond\ the\ boundary\ of\ the\ chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00446\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02950\ DRWAV\_PRIVATE\ drwav\_uint32\ drwav\_get\_bytes\_per\_pcm\_frame(\mbox{\hyperlink{structdrwav}{drwav}}*\ pWav)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02951\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02952\ \ \ \ \ drwav\_uint32\ bytesPerFrame;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02953\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02954\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02955\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ bytes\ per\ frame\ is\ a\ bit\ ambiguous.\ It\ can\ be\ either\ be\ based\ on\ the\ bits\ per\ sample,\ or\ the\ block\ align.\ The\ way\ I'm\ doing\ it\ here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02956\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ is\ that\ if\ the\ bits\ per\ sample\ is\ a\ multiple\ of\ 8,\ use\ floor(bitsPerSample*channels/8),\ otherwise\ fall\ back\ to\ the\ block\ align.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02957\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02958\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((pWav-\/>bitsPerSample\ \&\ 0x7)\ ==\ 0)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02959\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Bits\ per\ sample\ is\ a\ multiple\ of\ 8.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02960\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ bytesPerFrame\ =\ (pWav-\/>bitsPerSample\ *\ pWav-\/>fmt.channels)\ >>\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02961\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02962\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ bytesPerFrame\ =\ pWav-\/>fmt.blockAlign;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02963\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02964\ }
